\subsection{Detailed Description}
Contains the definitions of the Key-\/\-Value pairs. {\bfseries Project} 1814 I\-O\-Lab Remote Sensor Application

{\bfseries Description} Contains the definitions of the Key-\/\-Value pairs used for configuring the different sensors in the I\-O\-Lab system. The keys and values defined in this module are based on the document 1814\-F08 Data Protocol Key-\/\-Value table. 

Definition in file \hyperlink{_key_value_8h_source}{Key\-Value.\-h}.
